     <h2 class="intro" style="font-size: 3em;"> Select a Virtual Tour</h2> 
     <div class="grid_3 alpha"> 
      <a href="/VisitUCR/virtualCampusTour" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual campus tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/bellTower.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Campus</strong></h3> 
       <p>Get a great overview of campus. See our main academic buildings, libraries, Campus Store and more. </p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_3"> 
      <a href="/VisitUCR/virtualStudentLifeTour" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual student life tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/scottyCheer.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Student Life</strong></h3> 
       <p>See how our campus comes alive. Check out everything from the Highlander Union Building to the Student Recreation Center. </p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_3"> 
      <a href="/VisitUCR/virtualAcademicTour" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual academic tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/libraryInterior.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Academic</strong></h3> 
       <p>Get a sneak peek at the rooms you'll learn inside. From Rivera Library to the Insectary, you have a lot to look forward to!</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_3 omega"> 
      <a href="http://www.vpix.net/index.php?tour=103925" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual housing tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/campusApartment.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Housing</strong></h3> 
       <p>Take a closer look at the comfortable rooms in our residence halls, campus apartments and family housing communities.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div>

     <h2 class="intro" style="font-size: 3em;"> Select a Virtual Tour</h2> 
     <div class="grid_3 alpha"> 
      <a href="/VisitUCR/virtualCampusTour" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual campus tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/bellTower.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Campus</strong></h3> 
       <p>Get a great overview of campus. See our main academic buildings, libraries, Campus Store and more. </p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_3"> 
      <a href="/VisitUCR/virtualStudentLifeTour" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual student life tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/scottyCheer.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Student Life</strong></h3> 
       <p>See how our campus comes alive. Check out everything from the Highlander Union Building to the Student Recreation Center. </p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_3"> 
      <a href="/VisitUCR/virtualAcademicTour" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual academic tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/libraryInterior.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Academic</strong></h3> 
       <p>Get a sneak peek at the rooms you'll learn inside. From Rivera Library to the Insectary, you have a lot to look forward to!</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <div class="grid_3 omega"> 
      <a href="http://www.vpix.net/index.php?tour=103925" target="_blank"> <img alt="Take a virtual housing tour." class="spaceBottom1" width="160" height="215" src="/Images/virtualTours/campusApartment.jpg" /></a> 
      <div class="centerTxt"> 
       <h3 class="orange verd"> <strong>Housing</strong></h3> 
       <p>Take a closer look at the comfortable rooms in our residence halls, campus apartments and family housing communities.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div>

   <div id="content"> 
    <h2>Fees and Refunds</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/" title="Home">Home</a></li>
       <li><a href="/admin/community/" title="Community Engagement">Community Engagement</a></li>
       <li><a href="/cs/" title="Conferencing Services">Conferencing Services</a></li>
       <li><a href="/admin/about/" title="About UCR Extension">About UCR Extension</a></li>
       <li><a href="/instructors.html" title="Instructors">Instructors</a></li>
       <li><a href="" title=""></a></li>
       <li><a href="/academics/" title="Areas of Study">Areas of Study</a></li>
       <li><a href="/enroll/" title="Browse Courses">Browse Courses</a></li> 
      </ul> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <hr /> 
    <!-- End Sidebar --> 
    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <h3 class="brown_background"><img src="/images/admin/about_fees.gif" alt="About Fees" width="118" height="28" /><style class="accessibility">Fees</style></h3> 
      <h4>Course Fee</h4> 
      <ul> 
       <li>The fee for each course is listed on the course information page.</li> 
       <li>The fee listed for each course is the same for auditors as for credit students.</li> 
       <li>Course fees may be paid by either: 
        <ul> 
         <li>A check payable to Regents-UC.</li> 
         <li>Purchase order.</li> 
         <li>VISA or MasterCard.</li> 
        </ul> </li> 
      </ul> 
      <h4 class="section">Late Enrollment Fee</h4> 
      <p>A fee may be charged for enrollments received after the first class meeting. Please see the specific course's description or contact <a href="mailto:%20register@ucx.ucr.edu">Student Services</a> for more information.</p> 
      <h4 class="section">Returned Check Fee</h4> 
      <p>A $25 collection fee is required by the university.</p> 
      <h3 class="brown_background"><img src="/images/admin/about_refunds.gif" alt="About Refunds" width="145" height="28" /><style class="accessibility">About Refunts</style></h3> 
      <p>Full refunds are automatically processed for courses which have been cancelled or discontinued. All other refund requests must be in writing. Unless otherwise noted in the course description, refunds will be granted based on the following criteria:</p> 
      <ul> 
       <li>One- to three-day courses – A full refund will be granted if a request is received by the close of business the day prior to the first class session, after which no refunds are granted.</li> 
       <li>Courses with four or more meetings – A full refund will be granted if a request is received by the close of business the day prior to the first class session. A refund minus a $25 service charge and any nonrefundable materials fee will be granted if received the next business day following the first class session, after which no refunds are granted.</li> 
       <li>Alternate Refund Deadlines or Special Refund Policies apply to some courses. Please see the notes in the course description and/or contact Student Services for details. <br /> 
        <ul> 
         <li>Alternate Refund Deadlines: If a course has an alternate refund deadline, it is displayed in the course details fee area. These alternate dates are necessary due to up-front financial commitments relating to the specific course.</li> 
         <li>Special Refund Policy &quot;A&quot; (applies to Education's e-learning courses)<br />A full refund for all Education Extension e-Learning courses (online, hybrid, webcast, videoconference) will be issued only if received in writing 2 days prior to the start date of the course. Refund requests received after that date may be granted only on a case-by-case basis, upon review by the Director of Education Extension, and will be assessed a minimum $50 drop fee. NO refunds will be granted on or after the start date of the course.</li> 
         <li>Special Refund Policy &quot;B&quot; (applies to Forensic Nursing, Case Management and Legal Nurse Consulting)<br />If you decide to drop the course, a $50 fee will be withheld from the tuition refund. You must submit your request to drop in writing prior to the opening of the class or within seven days of your enrollment date. No refund will be granted if requested after the times indicated above. Please submit your written requests to <a href="mailto:register@ucx.ucr.edu ?subject=Refund%20Request">register@ucx.ucr.edu </a>or mail to: UCR Extension, 1200 University Ave., Riverside CA 92507</li> 
        </ul> </li> 
       <li>Concurrent course refund policy – Refunds are computed according to undergraduate and/or graduate course policies, which allow for partial refunds up to the fifth week of the course, after which no refunds are granted. <a href="/admin/student/concurrent.html">Visit our concurrent enrollment page to learn more</a>.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <div class="shaded_box top"> 
       <p><strong class="highlight">Mail refund requests to:</strong></p> 
       <address class="vcard"> <span class="fn org">UCR Extension<br /> University of California </span><br /> <span class="adr"> <span class="locality">Riverside</span>, <span class="region">CA</span> <span class="postal-code">92521-0112</span><br /> </span> or deliver in person to the UCR Extension Student Services Office. </address> 
       <p>Refunds will not be processed until written request is received. Allow three to six weeks processing time.</p> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div>

    <h2 class="long">News Releases</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/media/" title="Media Home">Media Home<br /><span>Partnering to tell UCR's story</span></a></li>

       <li><a href="/media/experts.html" title="Experts on Demand">Experts on Demand<br /><span>Find the perfect source</span></a></li>
       <li class="currentpage"><h3><dfn>Current page is: </dfn>News Releases</h3></li>

      </ul> 
     </div>

    <hr /> 
    <!-- End Sidebar --> 
    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <h3>What is Breaking at UCR?</h3> 
     <p>Sometimes instead of providing someone to comment on the news, <a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/">UC Riverside makes the news</a>. Our events and milestones may be UCR centered sometimes, but other times may offer clues to larger trends in higher education or world events.</p> 
     <div id="news_items"> 
      <img class="border_image" src="/media/images/releases_header.jpg" alt=" " width="484" height="97" /> 
      <h4 class="accessibility">News and Events</h4> 
      <!-- Feed accessed 2014-03-11T15:51:39-07:00--> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20966">Brain Awareness Day to Cover Sheep Brains, Cow Hearts, Scorpions and Zombie Cockroaches</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(March 11, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>Brain Awareness Day this year will take place on March 12 on the UC Riverside campus.</p> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20960">Susan Straight is a Southern California Original</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(March 10, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>Susan Straight, a native of Riverside and a longtime professor of creative writing at UC Riverside, will receive the Kirsch Award for lifetime achievement at the awards ceremony for the Los Angeles Times Book Prizes. The event is Friday, April 11 at the University of Southern California’s Bovard Auditorium.</p> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20897">UCR to Host Inaugural BlaqOUT Conference on April 18-19, 2014</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(March 7, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>The LGBT Resource Center at the University of California, Riverside will host the inaugural BlaqOUT Conference at the Highlander Union Building on April 18-19, 2014. The conference is for individuals who self-identify as Black/African American or of African descent and as Same Gender Loving, Lesbian, Gay, Bisexual, Transgender, Queer, Questioning or somewhere on the LGBT spectrum.</p> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20889">Gladys Eaton Dies at 92</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(March 4, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>Gladys M. Eaton, whose husband’s collection of science fiction books formed the basis of UC Riverside’s Eaton Collection of Science Fiction and Fantasy, died Jan. 22. She was 92.</p> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20879">Combining Forces to Stop Hackers</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(March 4, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>StopTheHacker, an anti-malware company created by a graduate of the University of California, Riverside Bourns College of Engineering, has been bought by CloudFlare, the web performance and security company who protects more than 1.5 million web sites and sees five percent of Internet traffic worldwide.</p> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20861">Century-old Music Mystery Solved</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(February 28, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>What happened to an unpublished opera written by Enrique Granados, one of Spain’s greatest composers, at the turn of the 20th century? After a 20-year quest, UCR's Walter Clark found and acquired the original copy of &quot;Maria del Carmen.&quot;</p> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20836">March 6 Seminar to Examine Military Rape and Public Policy</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(February 26, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>Brig. Gen. (Ret.) Loree Sutton, M.D., and Laurie Leitch, Ph.D. will discuss “Military Rape and Public Policy in Real Time?” in a March 6 seminar.</p> 
      <h5><a href="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/20732">UCR to Offer Free Parking For Visitors at Selected Events</a></h5> 
      <p><strong>(February 25, 2014)</strong></p> 
      <p>The University of California, Riverside will begin offering free parking for guests attending no-cost and selected low-cost events on campus as part of a new parking initiative that campus leadership hopes will encourage more community members to participate in academic, cultural and student programs and gatherings. The program was announced in a joint message from Chancellor Kim Wilcox and Executive Vice Chancellor/Provost Dallas Rabenstein Monday.</p> 
     </div> 
     <div id="news_archive"> 
      <h3><img id="pages" class="img_R_borderless" src="/media/images/3pages.png" alt="." width="65" height="68" />UCR Press Release Archive</h3> 
      <p> Looking for an older press release? Our <a href="http://newsroom.ucr.edu/news_archive.html">searchable archives page</a> has every electronic press release dating back to the 1998. Get the background or historical information you need right here. </p> 
     </div> 
    </div>

  <script>
    var ytpreload = ytpreload || {};
    ytpreload.SnapClassList = ['content-snap-width-1', 'content-snap-width-2',
                               'content-snap-width-3'];
    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };
    (function() {
      var htmlEl = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
      var classList = [htmlEl.className];
        if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle()) {
          classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS);
            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();
  </script>

     <h2 id="btf_title"><span class="accessibility">Below the Fold</span><img alt="" src="http://ucrtoday.ucr.edu/wp-content/themes/ucr-newsroom.1.20/images/ttl_below_the_fold.png" height="16" width="222" /></h2> 
     <div class="column23"> 
      <div id="widget_ucrnewsroom_faculty_profile-27" class="widget widget_faculty_profile">
       <h3>Faculty Profile | <strong>Health</strong></h3>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
